function selectTrack(track) {\n            // Update frequency controls\n            const controlsContainer = document.getElementById(\'frequencyControls\');\n            controlsContainer.innerHTML = \'\';\n\n            track.frequencies.forEach((freq, index) => {\n                const controlGroup = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                controlGroup.className = \'control-group\';\n                controlGroup.innerHTML = `\n                    <label for="freq${index}">Layer ${index + 1} (Hz)</label>\n                    <input type="number" Update status\n            document.getElementById(\'status\').textContent = `Selected: ${track.name}`;\n            document.getElementById(\'status\').className = \'status playing\';\n        }\n\n        // Start session\n        function startSession() {\n            if (isPlaying) {\n                stopSession();\n            }\n\n            try {\n                audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();\n                \n                const freqInputs = document.querySelectorAll(\'#frequencyControls input[type="number"]\');\n                const duration = parseInt(document.getElementById(\'duration\').value) * 60 * 1000;\n\n                oscillators = [];\n                gainNodes = [];\n\n                freqInputs.forEach((input, index) => {\n                    const freq = parseFloat(input.value);\n                    if (freq > 0) {\n                        const oscillator = audioContext.createOscillator();\n                        const gainNode = audioContext.createGain();\n\n                        oscillator.type = \'sine\';\n                        oscillator.frequency.setValueAtTime(freq, audioContext.currentTime);\n\n                        // Volume formula: 0.5 / (number of oscillators)\n                        const volume = 0.5 / freqInputs.length;\n                        gainNode.gain.setValueAtTime(0, audioContext.currentTime);\n                        gainNode.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(volume, audioContext.currentTime + 0.1);\n\n                        oscillator.connect(gainNode);\n                        gainNode.connect(audioContext.destination);\n\n                        oscillator.start();\n                        oscillators.push(oscillator);\n                        gainNodes.push(gainNode);\n                    }\n                });\n\n                isPlaying = true;\n                document.getElementById(\'status\').textContent = \'Session running...\';\n                document.getElementById(\'status\').className = \'status playing\';\n\n                // Auto-stop after duration\n                setTimeout(() => {\n                    if (isPlaying) {\n                        stopSession();\n                    }\n                }, duration);\n\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\'Error starting session:\', error);\n                alert(\'Error starting audio session. Please try again.\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Stop session\n        function stopSession() {\n            if (oscillators.length > 0) {\n                oscillators.forEach((osc, index) => {\n                    if (gainNodes[index]) {\n                        gainNodes[index].gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, audioContext.currentTime + 0.1);\n                    }\n                    setTimeout(() => {\n                        osc.stop();\n                    }, 100);\n                });\n            }\n\n            if (audioContext) {\n                audioContext.close();\n                audioContext = null;\n            }\n\n            oscillators = [];\n            gainNodes = [];\n            isPlaying = false;\n\n            document.getElementById(\'status\').textContent = \'Session stopped\';\n            document.getElementById(\'status\').className = \'status stopped\';\n        }\n\n        // Initialize on load\n        document.addEventListener(\'DOMContentLoaded\', init);\n    </script>\n</body>\n</html>\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

System\n```javascript\nclass FrequencyGenerator {\n    constructor() {\n        this.audioContext = null;\n        this.oscillators = [];\n        this.gainNodes = [];\n    }\n    \n    startSession(frequencies, duration) {\n        this.audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();\n        \n        frequencies.forEach((freq, index) => {\n            const oscillator = this.audioContext.createOscillator();\n            const gainNode = this.audioContext.createGain();\n            \n            oscillator.frequency.value = freq;\n            oscillator.type = \'sine\';\n            \n            // Volume formula: 0.5 / number of oscillators\n            const volume = 0.5 / frequencies.length;\n            gainNode.gain.value = volume;\n            \n            oscillator.connect(gainNode);\n            gainNode.connect(this.audioContext.destination);\n            \n            oscillator.start();\n            this.oscillators.push(oscillator);\n            this.gainNodes.push(gainNode);\n        });\n        \n        // Auto-stop after duration\n        setTimeout(() => this.stopSession(), duration * 60 * 1000);\n    }\n    \n    stopSession() {\n        this.oscillators.forEach((osc, index) => {\n            if (this.gainNodes[index]) {\n                this.gainNodes[index].gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, this.audioContext.currentTime + 0.1);\n            }\n            setTimeout(() => osc.stop(), 100);\n        });\n        \n        this.oscillators = [];\n        this.gainNodes = [];\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Gold Features:**\n- Clean class-based architecture\n- Proper cleanup of audio resources\n- Smooth fade-out (0.1s ramp)\n- oscillators[index].frequency.setValueAtTime(value, audioContext.currentTime);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Start session\n        function startSession() {\n            if (isPlaying) {\n                stopSession();\n            }\n\n            if (!currentTrack) {\n                alert(\'Please select a track first\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            try {\n                audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();\n                \n                const freqInputs = document.querySelectorAll(\'#frequencyControls input[type="number"]\');\n                const duration = parseInt(document.getElementById(\'duration\').value) * 60 * 1000;\n\n                oscillators = [];\n                gainNodes = [];\n\n                freqInputs.forEach((input, index) => {\n                    const freq = parseFloat(input.value);\n                    if (freq > 0) {\n                        const oscillator = audioContext.createOscillator();\n                        const gainNode = audioContext.createGain();\n\n                        oscillator.type = \'sine\';\n                        oscillator.frequency.setValueAtTime(freq, audioContext.currentTime);\n\n                        // Volume formula: 0.5 / (number of oscillators)\n                        const volume = 0.5 / freqInputs.length;\n                        gainNode.gain.setValueAtTime(0, audioContext.currentTime);\n                        gainNode.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(volume, audioContext.currentTime + 0.1);\n\n                        oscillator.connect(gainNode);\n                        gainNode.connect(audioContext.destination);\n\n                        oscillator.start();\n                        oscillators.push(oscillator);\n                        gainNodes.push(gainNode);\n                    }\n                });\n\n                isPlaying = true;\n                document.getElementById(\'status\').textContent = `Playing: ${currentTrack.name}`;\n                document.getElementById(\'status\').className = \'status playing\';\n\n                // Auto-stop after duration\n                setTimeout(() => {\n                    if (isPlaying) {\n                        stopSession();\n                    }\n                }, duration);\n\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\'Error starting session:\', error);\n                alert(\'Error starting audio session. Please try again.\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Stop session\n        function stopSession() {\n            if (oscillators.length > 0) {\n                oscillators.forEach((osc, index) => {\n                    if (gainNodes[index]) {\n                        gainNodes[index].gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, audioContext.currentTime + 0.1);\n                    }\n                    setTimeout(() => {\n                        osc.stop();\n                    }, 100);\n                });\n            }\n\n            if (audioContext) {\n                audioContext.close();\n                audioContext = null;\n            }\n\n            oscillators = [];\n            gainNodes = [];\n            isPlaying = false;\n\n            // Update play button state\n            if (currentTrack) {\n                const activeCard = document.querySelector(`[data-track-id="${currentTrack.id}"]`);\n                if (activeCard) {\n                    const playBtn = activeCard.querySelector(\'.play-btn\');\n                    if (playBtn) {\n                        playBtn.classList.remove(\'playing\');\n                        playBtn.textContent = \'\';\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            document.getElementById(\'status\').textContent = `Stopped: ${currentTrack ? currentTrack.name : \'Select a track\'}`;\n            document.getElementById(\'status\').className = \'status stopped\';\n        }\n\n        // Close modal when clicking outside\n        document.addEventListener(\'click\', function(event) {\n            const modal = document.getElementById(\'trackInfoModal\');\n            if (event.target === modal) {\n                closeTrackInfo();\n            }\n        });\n\n        // Initialize on load\n        document.addEventListener(\'DOMContentLoaded\', init);\n    </script>\n</body>\n</html>\n</full-file-rewrite>\n</function_calls>'}
